   vihitatvaghaṭitāṅgatvākhyāśreyassādhanatā- bhāvānnātivyāptiprasaṃgaḥ /	vihita-tva-Gawita-aFga-tva-AKya-aSreya-ssADana-tA BAvAt-na-ati-vyApti-prasaMgaH /
   ataevoktam vārtike --- "tasmādyānyeva śāstrāṇi vedamūlānatikramāt //	ataeva-uktam vArtike -- "tasmAt-yAni-eva SAstrANi veda-mUla-anatikramAt //
   avasthitāni taireva jñāto dharmaḥ phalapradaḥ /	avasTitAni tEH-eva jQAtaH DarmaH Pala-pradaH /
   " tathā --- "vedenaivābhyanujñātā yeṣāmeva pravaktṛtā //	" taTA -- "vedena-eva-aByanujQAtAH yezAm-eva pravaktRtA //
   nityānāmabhidheyānāṃ manvantarayugādiṣu /	nityAnAm-aBiDeyAnAm manvantara-yuga-Adizu /
   teṣāṃ viparivartteṣu kurvatāṃ dharmasaṃhitāḥ /	tezAm viparivarttezu kurvatAm Darma-saMhitAH /
   vacanāni pramāṇāni nānyeṣāmiti niścayaḥ /	vacanAni pramANAni na-anyezAm-iti niScayaH /
   " itīti, tattadadhikaraṇakaustubha eva dūṣitaṃ draṣṭavyam /	" iti-iti, tad-tad-aDikaraNa-kOstuBaH eva dUzitam drazwavyam /
   atra matāntaranirāsaḥ kaustubhe draṣṭavyaḥ /	atra mata-antara-nirAsaH kOstuBe drazwavyaH /
   tasmin pūrvoktamate anāśvāsāt pakṣāntaramāha - astuveti //	tasmin pUrva-ukta-mate anASvAsAt pakza-antaram-Aha  astuva-iti //
   nacaivaṃ prāmāṇyābhāve 'dhyāyāsaṃgatiḥ;	na-ca-evam prAmANya-aBAve aDyAya-asaMgatiH;
   arthavādopayogaprasaṃgādadhyāyāsaṅgatasyāpyarthasya nirūpaṇe bādhakābhāvāt	arTavAda-upayoga-prasaMgAt-aDyAya-asaFgatasya-api-arTasya nirUpaNe bADaka-aBAvAt
   sāṃgavedopayogasyaiva vā jijñāsitatvena adhyāyārthatvāṅgīkārādvā	sAMga-veda-upayogasya-eva vA jijQAsita-tvena aDyAya-arTa-tva-aFgIkArAt-vA
   mantrādhikaraṇasyopayogamātravicāraviṣayatvopapatterityarthaḥ //	mantra-aDikaraNasya-upayoga-mAtra-vicAra-vizaya-tva-upapatteH-iti-arTaH //
   prayojanamiti //	prayojanam-iti //
   yathā --- arthavādāvagatameva prāśastyaṃ	yaTA -- arTa-vAda-avagatam-eva prASastyam
   dharmapravṛttyupayogitayābhyudakāri, tathehāpi	Darma-pravRtti-upayogi-taya-aByudakAri, taTA-iha-api
   mantrajanyasmṛtirevābhyudayakāriṇīti prayojanamityarthaḥ /	mantra-janya-smRtiH-eva-aByudaya-kAriNI-iti prayojanam-iti-arTaH /
   tathā --- "agnihotrapadaṃ nāmā ghāre yāgakalpanam /	taTA -- "agnihotra-padam nAmA GAre yAga-kalpanam /
   mukhyārthe viniyogo 'yaṃ āmikṣā paya evace" tyādinoktāni prayojanāntarāṇi	muKya-arTe viniyogaH ayam AmikzA payaH eva-ced tyAdinA-uktAni prayojana-antarANi
   kaustubhe draṣṭavyānīti //	kOstuBe drazwavyAni-iti //
   iti	iti
   śrīmatpūrvottaramīmāṃsāpārāvāradhurīṇaśrīkhaṇḍadevāntevāsikavimaṇḍanabālakṛṣṇasutaśaṃbhubhaṭṭaviracitāyāṃ	SrImat-pUrva-uttara-mImAMsA-pArAvAra-DurINa-SrIKaNxa-deva-antevAsika-vi-maNxana-bAla-kRzNa-suta-SaMBu-Bawwa-viracitAyAm
   bhāṭṭadīpikāprabhāvalyāṃ prathamādhyāyasya dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ //	BAwwa-dIpikA-praBAvalyAm praTama-aDyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH //
